\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_tag}{Tag}} file parser.

Reads an XML-\/structured tagfile and builds up the structure in memory. The method \mbox{\hyperlink{classanonymous__namespace_02tagreader_8cpp_03_1_1_tag_file_parser_a9a2a4b0accaef9069229937226e60b10}{build\+Lists()}} is used to transfer/translate the structures to the doxygen engine. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2tagreader_8cpp_source_l00311}{311}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2tagreader_8cpp_source}{tagreader.\+cpp}}.
